## Analysis

The GT expression is:
$$f(x,v) = -1.68187 x^3 - 1.68187 x (0.04381 |v|^{1/3} + 1)$$

Expanding:
$$f(x,v) = -1.68187 x^3 - 1.68187 x - 0.07370 x |v|^{1/3}$$

This has three terms:
1. A term proportional to $x^3$
2. A term proportional to $x$
3. A term proportional to $x \cdot |v|^{1/3}$

The critical feature is the $x \cdot |v|^{1/3}$ term. Let me check each candidate for the ability to produce this term.

**Candidates with $v$ dependence:**
- **#2, #13, #17, #22, #27**: These contain $v$ linearly (e.g., $c_3 v + c_4 v$), not $|v|^{1/3}$. Cannot match.
- **#16**: Contains $v^2 x$, not $|v|^{1/3} x$. Cannot match.
- **#46**: Contains $v^2 x$, not $|v|^{1/3} x$. Cannot match.
- **#50**: Contains $x |x|^{1/3}$ and linear $v$ terms, not $x |v|^{1/3}$. Cannot match.

**Candidates without $v$ dependence:**
All remaining candidates are functions of $x$ only (and possibly $t$, but $t$ doesn't appear in GT either). However, the GT depends on $v$ through the $|v|^{1/3}$ term. Since none of these candidates include $v$ dependence, they cannot reproduce the GT for all values of both $x$ and $v$.

Specifically, the GT varies with $v$ (through $|v|^{1/3}$), so any candidate that is purely a function of $x$ will fail to match the GT across different values of $v$.

**No candidate** contains a term of the form $x \cdot |v|^{1/3}$ or any equivalent construction that could produce this dependence. Therefore, no candidate can be made equivalent to the GT.

Conclusion: No match
